                         <div data-reactid="3">
                          This is a quaint home that is comfy / cozy. We want you to experience a true retreat - your home away from home yet an escape from daily routine. At nearly 1,100 sq feet, it has gorgeous hardwood floors, two bedrooms, a living room, dining room, kitchen, and of course a bathroom. It is spacious for two but also comfortable for four, its maximum capacity. It does have a single "bath" but please note the picture of bathroom - it has a shower only. No tub.
                         </div>
                         <div data-reactid="4">
                          The neighborhood is in an older area of town and is typical of most older neighborhoods in Hot Springs. It is just off two major cross-town streets, so most everything is just minutes away.

Downstairs features another kitchen, den, two bedrooms (1 bedroom with 1 queen &amp; 1 bedroom with 2 queens) and a bath. The downstairs doors open to another covered patio and leads to the sidewalk to the water. Come here to enjoy all that Hot Springs has to offer from the lakes, beautiful Garvan Gardens, to the horse racing and gaming at Oaklawn Park. Just bring your clothes and leave your worries at home!

                         <div data-reactid="5">
                          <li data-reactid="6"><p data-reactid="7">Staying at Jenelle's place was like a trip back in time. The farmhouse is homey, spacious and reminded us each of our grandparents' homes, complete with a cozy kitchen and a great couch to enjoy iced tea and apple pie. The fridge and oven are original to the house, and so we were surprised that the ice maker in the fridge worked well and the oven was really cute and held the temperature well. The dishwasher (not original to the house) worked well. We only used one of the two kitchens. In the large dining room with a record player, the large windows overlook the front yard. The two back bedrooms are filled with an amazing quality of light throughout the day. It was a very peaceful home to live and work from. We, along with our two dogs, stayed at the farmhouse for six months!! Since it seemed funny to write a review each month, I'll make this one a long one. Jenelle is super responsive to questions and has excellent communication; we felt very well taken care of. Thanks, Jenelle! The house itself is set back from the road and had huge beautiful trees all through the front and back yard. In spring, daffodils appeared all through the yard. There are several large fenced areas for the dogs, and our two loved trying to catch the squirrels. If you are lucky, enough you will be able to see horses in the back pasture. The horses were only there for a month during our stay. On either side of the backyard, there are two sets of metal tables and chairs so you can eat outside, though you'll want bug spray in the summer. There is a grapevine growing along one of the fences, and as we were leaving (June) I was starting to see grapes forming. There are a small pond and a large field out at the back of the property, and we enjoyed many walks out there, and the dogs loved to have so much free space to run. It's a pretty quiet community, but if you are staying for a little while I highly recommend you keep an eye out for signs at the Civic Center and joining a local fish fry or another event, we found the local community very friendly. The internet, while on the slow side, was fast enough for me to have video (SENSITIVE CONTENTS HIDDEN) calls and stream Netflix. We found that having the router as high up as it could go, really helped the connection. The carport provided a good cover for our cars. We had no issues getting deliveries from amazon etc. We thoroughly enjoyed our stay at the house, and we were quite sad to leave. </p><span data-reactid="8">Lora</span><span data-reactid="9">2016-07-01T00:00:00Z</span></li>
